If the option is checked the map rotate with you, otherwise the map is always facing north.\r\n\r\n2) Follow me and draw route on the map. This way, if you go from point B to point A, you can follow a route on map previously stored and loaded (follow back).\r\n\r\n4) Replay route on the map (a route previously stored in step 2).
